### ­¤Ä© Arts & Cultural Opportunities

**City of West Hollywood 2026 Arts Grant Program**  
ŅłāThe City offers various grants for artists, including:Ņłä
- ŅłāArts Project Grant: Up to $20,000 for nonprofit arts organizations.Ņłä
- ŅłāCommunity Arts Grant: Up to $6,000 for individuals or nonprofits promoting BIPOC, LGBTQ+, and/or female artists.Ņłä
- ŅłāFilmmakers Grant: Up to $10,000 to support the completion of films already in post-production.Ņłä
- ŅłāTGI+ Arts Grant: Up to $6,500 for artists and nonprofits working with transgender, gender diverse, and intersex communities.Ņłä
- ŅłāWeHo Artist Grant: $6,000 annual grant for five local artists.Ņłä  
ŅłāApplication Deadline: July 1, 2025Ņłä  
­¤öŚ [Grant Details](https://wehoonline.com/west-hollywood-invites-applications-2026-arts-grants/)Ņłå
